### Intro Events ###
country_event = { #Ukraine in 1936
	id = ukraine.1
	title = ukraine.1.t
	desc = ukraine.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_opening
	trigger = {
		is_ai = no
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.1 option ukraine.1.a"
		name = ukraine.1.a
	}
}

### Lead-up to the Revolt ###

country_event = { # Dissent in the West
	id = ukraine.11
	title = ukraine.11.t
	desc = ukraine.11.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_farming

	option = { # Troubling
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.11 option ukraine.11.a"
		name = ukraine.11.a
		add_stability = -0.01
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukraine.12
				days = 2
				random = 120
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Tractor Factory Opens In Kyiv
	id = ukraine.12
	title = ukraine.12.t
	desc = ukraine.12.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_economy_growth
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # Great!
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.12 option ukraine.12.a"
		name = ukraine.12.a
		add_political_power = 30
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine.13 days = 2 } # Strikes In Odesa
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Strikes In Odesa
	id = ukraine.13
	title = ukraine.13.t
	desc = ukraine.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_strike
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = ukraine.14 # Rally in Rivne
				days = 2
				random = 120
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Give empty promises
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.13 option ukraine.13.a"
		name = ukraine.13.a

		add_political_power = -15
		add_stability = -0.01
	}

	option = { # Send police
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.13 option ukraine.13.b"
		name = ukraine.13.b

		add_political_power = -5
		add_stability = -0.03
	}
}

country_event = { # Rally in Rivne
	id = ukraine.14
	title = ukraine.14.t
	desc = ukraine.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_HOL_syndicalist_rally
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.14 option ukraine.14.a"
		name = ukraine.14.a #Have Petlyura arrested
		ai_chance = { factor = 65 }
		add_stability = 0.01
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine.15 days = 2 } # Petlyura evades arrest
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.14 option ukraine.14.b"
		name = ukraine.14.b #Leave Him
		ai_chance = { factor = 35 }
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_petliura_left_alone
	}
}

country_event = { # Black Monday Hits Ukraine!
	id = ukraine.16
	title = ukraine.16.t
	desc = ukraine.16.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_run_on_the_banks
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { # We still have time
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.16 option ukraine.16.a"
		name = ukraine.16.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_ideas = UKR_black_monday
		set_variable = { UKR_BM_length = 500 }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_relief.1 days = 18 } # Start of Relief Bill negotiations
			country_event = { id = ukraine.17 days = 60 } # Formation of VDR
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Severity of protests increases in August
	id = ukraine.25
	title = ukraine.25.t
	desc = {
		text = ukraine.25.d1
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_bill_failed }
	}
	desc = {
		text = ukraine.25.d2
		trigger = { has_country_flag = UKR_bill_sucessfull }
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_BEL_Hainaut_Liberated
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.25 option ukraine.25.a"
		name = ukraine.25.a
		add_stability = -0.05
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_bill_failed }	# Bill failed, Soim is seen as unreliable
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine.26 days = 3 } # SHD approaches Hetman about martial law
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Appointment of Supreme Otaman
	id = ukraine.35
	title = ukraine.35.t
	desc = ukraine.35.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_diplomacy1

	option = { #prisovskyi
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.35 option ukraine.35.a"
		name = ukraine.35.a
		trigger = { has_character = UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi }
		UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
	}
	option = { #konovalets
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.35 option ukraine.35.b"
		name = ukraine.35.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_government = national_populist }
		}
		UKR_yevhen_konovalets = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
	}
	option = { #Melynk as Konovalets' replacement
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.35 option ukraine.35.b2"
		name = ukraine.35.b2
		trigger = {
			has_government = national_populist
		}
		UKR_andrii_melnyk = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
		add_political_power = 50
	}
	option = { #ivan p-o
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.35 option ukraine.35.c"
		name = ukraine.35.c
		trigger = { has_character = UKR_ivan_poltavets_ostrianytsia }
		UKR_ivan_poltavets_ostrianytsia = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
	}
	option = { #zahrodskyi as prisovskyi's replacement
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.35 option ukraine.35.e"
		name = ukraine.35.e
		trigger = { NOT = { has_character = UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi } }
		UKR_oleksandr_zahrodskyi = {
			promote_leader = yes
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_trait = organizer } }
				add_unit_leader_trait = organizer
			}
			add_unit_leader_trait = expert_delegator
			add_planning = 1
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Nation at war
	id = ukraine.58
	title = ukraine.58.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = no
			is_monarchy = yes
			has_war_with = RUS
			RUS = {
				has_elected_government = yes
				is_monarchy = no
			}
		}
		text = ukraine.58.d1 #hetmanate vs democratic RUS
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_elected_government = yes
			has_war_with = RUS
			RUS = {
				has_elected_government = yes
				is_monarchy = no
			}
		}
		text = ukraine.58.d2 #democratic UKR vs democratic RUS
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_war_with = SOV
			UKR = {
				has_elected_government = no
				is_monarchy = yes
			}
		}
		text = ukraine.58.d3 #hetmanate vs socialist RUS
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_war_with = SOV }
				OR = {
					has_elected_government = yes
					is_monarchy = no
				}
			}
			else = {
				OR = {
					RUS = { has_elected_government = no }
					is_monarchy = yes
					AND = {
						has_elected_government = no
						is_monarchy = no
					}
				}
			}
		}
		text = ukraine.58.d4 #generic
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_war_with = RUS
			has_war_with = SOV
		}
		NOT = { has_government = syndicalist }
	}

	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_towar

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.58 option ukraine.58.a"
		name = ukraine.58.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				RUS = {
					has_elected_government = yes
					is_monarchy = no
				}
				UKR = {
					has_elected_government = no
					is_monarchy = yes
				}
			}
			add_war_support = 0.10
		}
		else = {
			add_war_support = 0.15
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = syndicalist
					has_government = radical_socialist
					has_government = social_democrat
					has_government = social_liberal
					has_government = national_populist
				}
			}
			UKR_oleksii_fedorov = { set_nationality = UKR }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					UKR = { is_ai = no }
				}
				play_song = ukraine_is_not_yet_lost
			}
		}
	}
}

	title = ukraine.60.t
	desc = ukraine.60.d

	fire_only_once = yes

		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.60 option ukraine.60.a"
		name = ukraine.60.a

			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_danylo_skoropadskyi } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = -0.05
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = UKR_record_grain_sales
				days = 365
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_volodymyr_vynnychenko } }
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = -0.03
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = -0.03
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = UKR_record_grain_sales
				days = 365
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = -5 }
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = UKR_record_grain_sales
				days = 365
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.60 option ukraine.60.b"
		name = ukraine.60.b
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = UKR_danylo_skoropadskyi }
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = UKR_volodymyr_vynnychenko }
			}
			add_stability = 0.05
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.05
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.05
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_stability = 0.05
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 10 }
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		}
	}
}

		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_protofis_support_decrease_slight

		add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_support = -10 }

			}

		}

		}
	}

		name = ukraine_relief.2.b

		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_protofis_support_increase_slight

		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_banking_curves_nationalisation_tt

		add_to_variable = { UKR_protofis_support = 10 }

			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = { id = ukraine_relief.3 days = 5 } # Bank crash
				}
				50 = {

				}
			}
		}
	}

		clear_variable = UKR_udkhp_support

		remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_URDP target = THIS }
		remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_independents target = THIS }

country_event = { # End of the Relief Bill negotiations
	id = ukraine_relief.100
	title = ukraine_relief.100.t
	desc = ukraine_relief.100.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_protofis target = THIS }
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_URDP target = THIS }
			remove_targeted_decision = { decision = UKR_negotiate_with_independents target = THIS }
			remove_mission = UKR_bill_negotiations
			clr_country_flag = UKR_protofis_stalls_negotiations
			clr_country_flag = UKR_defection_of_independents
			clr_country_flag = UKR_SHD_influence_flag
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_doroshenko

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief.100 option ukraine_relief.100.a"
		name = ukraine_relief.100.a # failure
		trigger = {
			check_variable = { UKR_bill_success < 4 }
		}
		remove_ideas = UKR_black_monday
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_black_monday_recovery
			days = 500
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_bill_failed
		clr_country_flag = UKR_bill_negotiations_flag
		clear_variable = UKR_BM_length
		clear_variable = UKR_independents_support
		clear_variable = UKR_urdp_support
		clear_variable = UKR_protofis_support
		clear_variable = UKR_uskhd_support
		clear_variable = UKR_udkhp_support
		clear_variable = UKR_bill_success
		add_to_variable = { UKR_vdr_strength = 5 }
		subtract_from_variable = { UKR_hetman_strength = 5 }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_relief.100 option ukraine_relief.100.b"
		name = ukraine_relief.100.b #success
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				var = UKR_bill_success
				value = 4
				compare = greater_than_or_equals
			}
		}
		remove_ideas = UKR_black_monday
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_black_monday_recovery
			days = UKR_BM_length
		}
		add_stability = 0.1
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { UKR_bill_success = 4 } } # success
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = UKR_relief_bill_passed
				days = UKR_BM_length
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_timed_idea = { # overwhelming success
				idea = UKR_relief_bill_passed_2
				days = UKR_BM_length
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_bill_sucessfull
		clr_country_flag = UKR_bill_negotiations_flag
		if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { UKR_protofis_support < 70 } }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_relief.101 days = 10 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine.34 days = 5 } # Hetman speeks in the Soim
		}
	}
}

			792 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
			199 = { set_demilitarized_zone = yes }
			GER = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.109 days = 2 } # Event informing about the start of revolt, for GER
			}
			set_variable = { UKR_authdem_foci = 0 }
			set_variable = { UKR_pataut_foci = 0 }
			set_country_flag = UKR_revolt_started #look here
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			country_lock_all_division_template = yes
			set_variable = { UKR_RP_intervention_time = 90 }
			set_variable = { UKR_reinforcement_time = 35 }
			set_variable = { UKR_rebel_attack_time = 14 }
			GER = { country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.14 days = 32 } }
			if = {
				limit = { GAL = { is_ai = no } }
				GAL = { country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.15 days = 12 } }
			}
			else = {
				AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.15 days = 12 } }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_revolt.1 option ukraine_revolt.1.a"
		name = ukraine_revolt.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 45
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_RADSOC }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SYNDIE }
				}
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_hetman_side_tt
		set_country_flag = UKR_hetman_side
		complete_national_focus = UKR_flames_of_rebellion
		add_ideas = UKR_anti_hetman_revolt
		set_variable = { UKR_vdr_strength = 25 }
		set_variable = { UKR_pacification_cost = 10 }
		activate_mission = UKR_rebel_attack
		activate_mission = UKR_odessa_in_flames
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.2 days = 1 }
			country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.4 days = 5 } #Rebels secure west
		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }
			country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.52 days = 153 } #If AI can't win revolt by February, autowin it
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_revolt.1 option ukraine_revolt.1.b"
		name = ukraine_revolt.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 55
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_USKHD_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_UDKHP_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_PATAUT }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_NATPOP }
					has_country_flag = UKR_hetman_side_ai
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_vdr_side
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_vdr_side_tt
		complete_national_focus = UKR_flames_of_rebellion
		add_ideas = UKR_anti_hetman_revolt
		set_variable = { UKR_hetman_strength = 75 }
		activate_mission = UKR_RP_intervention_mission
		activate_mission = UKR_borotbist_uprising
		hidden_effect = {

			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = { is_ai = yes }
				}

					10 = { country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.13 days = 10 random_days = 10 } } #Bombing of Sarny
					10 = { }

		}
		if = {
			limit = { is_ai = yes }

			}

			}
		}

			activate_mission = UKR_eastern_reinforcements_good

				limit = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }

			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		}

			country_event = { id = ukraine_revolt.11 days = 10 } #Traitors in VDR
		}
	}

###Land Reform and Industrialisation
country_event = { # Beginning of Land Reform/Industry Mission
	id = ukraine_landreform.1
	title = ukraine_landreform.1.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_pavlo_skoropadskyi } }
		text = ukraine_landreform.1.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_left_democratic_government = yes
			NOT = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_danylo_skoropadskyi } }
		}
		text = ukraine_landreform.1.d2
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_country_leader = { character = UKR_danylo_skoropadskyi } }
		text = ukraine_landreform.1.d3
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_farming

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_landreform.1 option ukraine_landreform.1.a"
		name = ukraine_landreform.1.a
		set_country_flag = UKR_land_reform_in_progress
		set_country_flag = UKR_industrialisation_in_progress
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = UKR_landreform_category
		activate_mission = UKR_landreform_mission
		unlock_decision_category_tooltip = UKR_industrialisation_category
		activate_mission = UKR_industrialisation_mission
		set_variable = { UKR_reform_in_progress = 0 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_government = authoritarian_democrat
					has_government = paternal_autocrat
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_shd.14 days = 15 }
				country_event = { id = ukraine_lun.20 days = 30 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_radicals_may_take_over_natpop_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_radicals_may_take_over_syndicalist_tt
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_industrial_score > 0 }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_industrialisation_current_tt
		}
	}
}

		name = ukraine_landreform.29.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_leader = { character = UKR_volodymyr_vynnychenko }
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.015
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.015
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 3 }
			change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = ukraine_coalition.70
	title = ukraine_coalition.70.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_justice_at_last }
		text = ukraine_coalition.70.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_reject_partisanship }
		text = ukraine_coalition.70.d2
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_WHR_sojm_meeting

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_coalition.70 option ukraine_coalition.70.a"
		name = ukraine_coalition.70.a #Succesfull parliamentarization
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_justice_at_last }
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_leader_portrait = {
				ideology = social_conservative
				portrait = GFX_IMAGE_NAME
			}
			set_portraits = {
				character = UKR_pavlo_skoropadskyi
				civilian = { large = gfx/leaders/UKR/Portrait_UKR_Pavlo_Skoropadskyi_Civilian.png }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { UKR_mykola_mikhnovskyi = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			activate_advisor = UKR_volodymyr_korostovets_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { UKR_volodymyr_korostovets = { is_second_in_command = yes } }
			activate_advisor = UKR_mykola_mikhnovskyi_sic
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.2
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine.68 days = 365 } #Pavlo Dies, Danylo Succeeds
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_coalition.70 option ukraine_coalition.70.b"
		name = ukraine_coalition.70.b #Failure
		trigger = { has_completed_focus = UKR_reject_partisanship }
		activate_advisor = UKR_oleksandr_shapoval_sic
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_liberal
			popularity = 0.04
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine.68 days = 365 } #Pavlo Dies, Danylo Succeeds
		}
	}
}

		set_variable = { UKR_ivan_mission_days_timeout = 75 }

		add_ideas = UKR_ivan_po_influence_idea_1
		hidden_effect = {
			activate_mission = UKR_ivan_po_mission
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = ROOT decision = UKR_solidfy_homzyn_position }
			country_event = { id = ukraine_shd.12 days = 80 random_days = 120 }
		}
	}

country_event = { #Question of USKhD and UDKhP
	id = ukraine_shd.3
	title = ukraine_shd.3.t
	desc = ukraine_shd.3.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_hetmanist_symbol
	trigger = { has_government = paternal_autocrat }

	option = { #Fully integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_shd.3 option ukraine_shd.3.a"
		name = ukraine_shd.3.a
		add_stability = -0.10
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_integrate_organisations_full
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }

			set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = UKR_new_pataut }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = sum } #avoid rounding errors

			set_popularities = {
				totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
				syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
				radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
				social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
				social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
				market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
				social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = 0
				paternal_autocrat = UKR_new_pataut
				national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
			country_event = { id = ukraine_shd.7 days = 35 }
		}
	}
	option = { #Somewhat integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_shd.3 option ukraine_shd.3.b"
		name = ukraine_shd.3.b
		add_stability = -0.05
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_integrate_organisations_half
		hidden_effect = {
			set_temp_variable = { UKR_new_authdem = UKR.party_popularity_100@authoritarian_democrat }
			divide_temp_variable = { UKR_new_authdem = 2 }

			set_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = UKR.party_popularity_100@paternal_autocrat }
			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = UKR_new_authdem }

			set_temp_variable = { sum = 100 }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@totalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_democrat }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@market_liberal }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@social_conservative }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = UKR_new_authdem }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = UKR_new_pataut }
			subtract_from_temp_variable = { sum = party_popularity_100@national_populist }

			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_new_pataut = sum } #avoid rounding errors

			set_popularities = {
				totalist = party_popularity_100@totalist
				syndicalist = party_popularity_100@syndicalist
				radical_socialist = party_popularity_100@radical_socialist
				social_democrat = party_popularity_100@social_democrat
				social_liberal = party_popularity_100@social_liberal
				market_liberal = party_popularity_100@market_liberal
				social_conservative = party_popularity_100@social_conservative
				authoritarian_democrat = UKR_new_authdem
				paternal_autocrat = UKR_new_pataut
				national_populist = party_popularity_100@national_populist
			}
			country_event = { id = ukraine_shd.7 days = 35 }
		}
	}
	option = { #Don't integrate
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_shd.3 option ukraine_shd.3.c"
		name = ukraine_shd.3.c
		add_stability = 0.06
	}
}

country_event = { #RadSoc Failure
	id = ukraine_republican.39
	title = ukraine_republican.39.t
	desc = ukraine_republican.39.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_vynnychenko_hryhoriiv
	trigger = {
		has_country_flag = UKR_GER_revbloc
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_republican.39 option ukraine_republican.39.a"
		name = ukraine_republican.39.a

		hidden_effect = {
			remove_country_leader_role = {
				character = UKR_volodymyr_vynnychenko
				ideology = social_democrat_subtype
			}
		}

		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = UKR_labor_principle }
			remove_ideas = UKR_labor_principle
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = UKR_labor_principle2 }
			remove_ideas = UKR_labor_principle2
		}

		add_ideas = UKR_minority_government

		add_popularity = {
			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.10
		}

		hidden_effect = {
			complete_national_focus = UKR_ascension_of_the_workers_party
			remove_mission = UKR_institute_progressive_labor_laws

			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = UKR_fight_and_you_will_overcome
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_revbloc_collapse

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_socialist_nationalization }

			clr_country_flag = UKR_socialist_nationalization
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_remove_socialist_nationalization
		}
	}
}

			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
			remove_from_coalition = yes
		}
		add_political_power = -75
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_liberal popularity = -0.03 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = -0.03 }
		set_country_flag = UKR_coalition_collapse
		add_ideas = UKR_minority_government
	}

		}

		}

			limit = { has_idea = UKR_labor_principle2 }
			remove_ideas = UKR_labor_principle2
		}

			ideology = radical_socialist
			popularity = -0.15
		}

			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = -0.10
		}

			complete_national_focus = UKR_ascension_of_the_workers_party
			remove_mission = UKR_institute_progressive_labor_laws

			uncomplete_national_focus = {
				focus = UKR_fight_and_you_will_overcome
				uncomplete_children = yes
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_revbloc_collapse

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_socialist_nationalization }

			clr_country_flag = UKR_socialist_nationalization
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_remove_socialist_nationalization
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Bloc lets Borotbists into Parliament, They jointly dissolve it
	id = ukraine_borotbist.20
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: ukraine_borotbist.20" }
	title = ukraine_borotbist.20.t
	desc = ukraine_borotbist.20.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_UKR_oleksandr_shumskyi
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_borotbist.20 option ukraine_borotbist.20.a"
		name = ukraine_borotbist.20.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = syndicalist
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		UKR_symon_petliura = { retire = yes }
		UKR_mykhailo_omelianovych_pavlenko = { retire = yes }
		UKR_kostiantyn_prisovskyi = { retire = yes }
		UKR_omelian_volokh = { promote_leader = yes }
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		activate_advisor = UKR_mykhailo_poloz_sic
		remove_ideas = UKR_syndie_general_strike
		remove_ideas = UKR_confused_army
		leave_faction = yes
		UKR_update_military = yes
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_military_access_to = UKR
				is_in_faction_with = GER
			}
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = PREV
				relation = military_access
				active = no
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_borotbysts_ukapist_bakhmut_pact
			}
			add_ideas = UKR_shaky_cooperation
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbist.72 days = 6 }
			}
		}
		UKR_syndie_revolution_angry_constitution = yes
		UKR_clear_republic_ideas = yes
		complete_national_focus = UKR_fighters_til_the_end
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_borotbyst_popularity_mechanic_tt
		set_temp_variable = { UKR_syndie_bonus = UKR.party_popularity_100@syndicalist }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = UKR_bakhmut_meeting_agree_to_ukapist
			}
			add_to_temp_variable = { UKR_syndie_bonus = UKR.party_popularity_100@totalist }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_syndie_bonus > 30 }
				has_country_flag = UKR_bakhmut_meeting_agree_to_ukapist
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_popular_revolution_tt
			add_ideas = UKR_revolutionary_might
			add_ideas = UKR_petliurites5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { UKR_syndie_bonus > 14 }
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = UKR_bakhmut_meeting_agree_to_ukapist
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_medium_popular_revolution_tt
			add_stability = 0.1
			add_political_power = 50
			add_ideas = UKR_petliurites3
		}
		else = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_unpopular_revolution_tt
			add_ideas = UKR_unpopular_revolution
			add_ideas = UKR_petliurites1
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
		add_timed_idea = {
			idea = UKR_economic_standstill
			days = 365
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_economic_crisis_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_leave_mitteleuropa = yes
			GER = { end_puppet = UKR }
			set_cosmetic_tag = UKR_republic
			country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbist.21 days = 3 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = { exists = yes }
					GER = {
						NOT = { has_war_with = RUS }
					}
				}
				GER = { country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbist.100 days = 5 } } #Decision to attack Ukrain
				RUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbist.100 days = 5 } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							UKR = { has_country_flag = POL_UKR_partition }
							UKR = { has_country_flag = POL_UKR_everything }
						}
					}
					AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbist.100 days = 5 } }
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = { exists = yes }
					GER = {
						NOT = { has_war_with = SOV }
					}
				}
				GER = { country_event = { id = ukraine_forpol.32 days = 5 } }
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							UKR = { has_country_flag = POL_UKR_partition }
							UKR = { has_country_flag = POL_UKR_everything }
						}
					}
					AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_forpol.32 days = 5 } }
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = SOV decision = UKR_join_moscow }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					RUS = {
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = UKR
						NOT = { is_in_faction_with = RUS }
					}
					white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
				}
				GER = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = UKR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							UKR = { has_country_flag = POL_UKR_partition }
							UKR = { has_country_flag = POL_UKR_everything }
							AND = {
								AUS = { NOT = { has_war_with = UKR } }
							}
						}
					}
					AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_forpol.32 days = 5 } }
				}
				add_ideas = UKR_fighters_till_the_end
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					SOV = {
						has_war_with = GER
					}
				}
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						has_war_with = UKR
					}
					white_peace_with_ROOT = yes
				}
				GER = {
					declare_war_on = {
						target = UKR
						type = annex_everything
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							UKR = { has_country_flag = POL_UKR_partition }
							UKR = { has_country_flag = POL_UKR_everything }
						}
						AUS = { NOT = { has_war_with = UKR } }
					}
					AUS = { country_event = { id = ukraine_forpol.32 days = 5 } }
				}
				activate_targeted_decision = { target = SOV decision = UKR_join_moscow }
			}
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			country_event = { id = ukraine_borotbist.73 days = 3 }
			set_country_flag = UKR_dont_attack_normally
			hidden_effect = {
				news_event = { id = ukraine_borotbist.200 days = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = UKR
		has_socialist_government = yes

			exists = yes
			surrender_progress < 0.1
		}

			any_neighbor_country = {
				OR = {
					tag = INT

					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {

		name = ukraine_borotbist.115.a

		}

			SOV = { add_to_faction = UKR }
		}
		UKR_update_military = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_government = syndicalist }
			activate_advisor = UKR_andrii_khvylia_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = radical_socialist }
			activate_advisor = UKR_volodymyr_chekhivskyi_sic
		}
		get_current_government_type = yes
		SOV = {

				target = UKR
				autonomy_state = kr_autonomous_puppet
			}
		}
		restore_previous_government_type = yes
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 7 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		remove_ideas = UKR_economic_standstill
		227 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		228 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = industrial_complex
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
		218 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1

				instant_build = yes
			}

		}
	}

### Ukraine forpol (negotiations with Germany)
country_event = { #for GER, start negotiations with Ukraine
	id = ukraine_forpol.15
	title = ukraine_forpol.15.t
	desc = {
		trigger = { UKR = { has_government = national_populist } }
		text = ukraine_forpol.15.lun.d
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = { UKR = { has_government = social_democrat } }
		text = ukraine_forpol.15.unr.b
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_forpol.15 option ukraine_forpol.15.a"
		name = ukraine_forpol.15.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				OR = {
					AND = {
						UKR = { has_government = national_populist }
						GER = { has_authoritarian_government = yes }
					}
					AND = {
						UKR = { has_government = social_democrat }
						GER = { has_left_democratic_government = yes }
					}
				}
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 2
				UKR = { has_government = social_democrat }
				WHR = { has_government = social_democrat }
			}
		}
		add_popularity = { ideology = social_democrat popularity = 0.01 }
		UKR = { country_event = { id = ukraine_forpol.16 days = 2 } }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_forpol.15 option ukraine_forpol.15.b"
		name = ukraine_forpol.15.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		add_popularity = { ideology = authoritarian_democrat popularity = 0.01 }
		UKR = {
			country_event = { id = ukraine_forpol.17 days = 2 }
			set_country_flag = UKR_GER_harsh
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Ukrainian counter-proposal
	id = ukraine_forpol.18
	title = ukraine_forpol.18.t
	desc = ukraine_forpol.18.d
	is_triggered_only = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #Accept
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_forpol.18 option ukraine_forpol.18.a"
		name = ukraine_forpol.18.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 10
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				UKR = { has_government = national_populist }
				GER = { has_authoritarian_government = yes }
			}
			modifier = {
				factor = 10
				UKR = { has_government = social_democrat }
				GER = { has_left_democratic_government = yes }
			}
		}
		UKR = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_harsh }
				clr_country_flag = UKR_GER_harsh
			}
			else = {
				set_country_flag = UKR_GER_compromise
			}
			country_event = { id = ukraine_forpol.19 days = 2 }
		}
	}
	option = { #Deny
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_forpol.18 option ukraine_forpol.18.b"
		name = ukraine_forpol.18.b
		ai_chance = { base = 20 }
		set_temp_variable = { ideology_change_var = 2 }
		change_ruling_party_popularity = yes
		UKR = { country_event = { id = ukraine_forpol.20 days = 2 } }
	}
}

		separate_peace_all_wars = yes
		AUS = { add_to_faction = UKR }
		UKR_update_military = yes
		set_country_flag = UKR_joined_DA
		GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = GER
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
				UKR = { give_military_access = PREV }
			}
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						tag = GER
						is_in_faction_with = GER
					}
				}
				PREV = { give_military_access = UKR }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			AUS = { country_event = ukraine_forpol.23 }
			GER = { country_event = ukraine_forpol.23 }
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		}

	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_forpol.23 option ukraine_forpol.23.b"
		name = ukraine_forpol.23.b
		trigger = { NOT = { tag = UKR } }
		if = {
			limit = { tag = AUS }
			add_political_power = 50
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			AUS = { add_to_faction = UKR }
			UKR = {
				GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
				add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #GER-UKR deal
	id = ukraine_forpol.25
	title = ukraine_forpol.25.t
	desc = ukraine_forpol.25.d
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_forpol.25 option ukraine_forpol.25.a"
		name = ukraine_forpol.25.a
		trigger = { tag = UKR }
		GER = { add_to_faction = UKR }
		GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
		add_to_tech_sharing_group = german_research
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_compromise } #Most lenient deal
			add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_harsh } #Strictest deal
			add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_3
			add_to_variable = { UKR_landreform_cost = 15 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_increase_reform_cost_15
		}
		else = { #Moderate deal
			add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_2
			add_to_variable = { UKR_landreform_cost = 10 }
			custom_effect_tooltip = UKR_increase_reform_cost_10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER = { country_event = ukraine_forpol.25 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine_forpol.25 option ukraine_forpol.25.a"
		name = ukraine_forpol.25.a
		trigger = { tag = GER }
		add_political_power = 50
		effect_tooltip = {
			UKR = {
				GER_add_to_mitteleuropa = yes
				add_to_tech_sharing_group = german_research
				GER = { add_to_faction = UKR }
				if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_compromise } #Most lenient deal
					add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_1
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_country_flag = UKR_GER_harsh } #Strictest deal
					add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_3
				}
				else = { #Moderate deal
					add_ideas = UKR_GER_deal_2
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Hidden AI event for going radical paths
	id = ukraine.1000
	title = ukraine.999.t
	desc = ukraine.999.b
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = { #LUN coup will not happen
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.1000 option 1"
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = UKR_pavlo_skoropadskyi }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 85
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_NATPOP }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #LUN coup will happen
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.1000 option 2"
		trigger = {
			has_country_leader = { character = UKR_pavlo_skoropadskyi }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 15
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_USKHD_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_UDKHP_AUTDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_PATAUT }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_ai_lun_coup
	}
	option = { #Borotbyst revolution will not happen
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.1000 option 3"
		trigger = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = UKR_republic
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 90
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SYNDIE }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Borotbyst revolution will happen
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event ukraine.1000 option 4"
		trigger = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = UKR_republic
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 5
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SOCLIB }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = UKR_path option = UKR_PATH_RADSOC }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = UKR_ai_borotbyst_revolution
	}
